***chrysalis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a> (94600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρυσαλλίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrusallís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρυσός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrusós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because of the color of some of them.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chrysalises</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chrysalides</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The pupa of a butterfly or moth, enclosed inside a <a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a>, in which metamorphosis <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> place
<ul><li><b>1929</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/M._Barnard_Eldershaw" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:M. Barnard Eldershaw">M. Barnard Eldershaw</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_House_Is_Built" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A House Is Built">A House <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> Built</a></i>, Chapter VII, Section viii
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>Fanny</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> afraid. She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> like an insect new-hatched from its <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></b>, naked and unprotected in a dawn she could not face.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a> itself.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A strong constraint.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">However, with the dainty volume my quondam friend sprang into fame. At the same time he cast off the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></b> of a commonplace existence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body> 
***chrysant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chrysant.html>chrysant</a> (132541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">chrysanthemum</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chubs</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One of various species of freshwater fish of the Cyprinidae or carp family, especially:
<ol><li>A European <a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a> (<i>Squalius cephalus</i>, syn. <i>Leuciscus cephalus</i>)</li>
<li>in Europe, its close relatives, notably the fallfish.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of various vaguely related marine or freshwater <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a>.
<ol><li>in North America, the black bass.</li></ol></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></i>.
</p>

***chubby.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a> (40964)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Recorded since 1611, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">short, thick fish species used as bait"; used metaphorically since 1558 for "lazy person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an assibilated form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cub</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a lump, heap, mass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cob</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*cubbe</i> (found only in derivative <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cubbel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a block to which an animal <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> tethered</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kubbr</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kumbr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">block, stump, log</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kumben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stumpy.html>stumpy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Cognate with dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">kubbug</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fat, plump, <a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chub.html>chub</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">chubbier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">chubbiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a person, slightly overweight, somewhat fat, and hence soft, plump, and rounded.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Marsha Hubler, <i>The Long Ride Home</i>, Zonderkidz (→ISBN), page 97:
<dl><dd>Slowly <a href = vnd.unilang:skye.html>Skye</a> wrapped her arms around the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></b> woman | s frame and rested her  head on <a href = vnd.unilang:rita.html>Rita</a> | s chest drenched with perspiration.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Obviously the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></b> child <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> eating too much.</i></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">chunky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">plump</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">podgy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tubby.html>tubby</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Of a body part, containing a moderate amount of fat.
<dl><dd><i>It's quite normal for <a href = vnd.unilang:babies.html>babies</a> to have <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></b> cheeks.</i></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">chunky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">plump</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">podgy</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***chutzpah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a> (94593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originated 1890–95 from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">חוצפּה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khutspe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Mishnaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חֻצְפָּה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khutspá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חָצַף</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khatsáf</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be insolent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aramaic" class="extiw" title="w:Aramaic">Aramaic</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">חוצפא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḥuṣpāʾ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">חֲצַף</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḥaṣap</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be insolent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">chutzpahs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Nearly <a href = vnd.unilang:arrogant.html>arrogant</a> courage; utter audacity, effrontery or impudence; supreme self-confidence; exaggerated self-opinion.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> January 22,  “Modern Manners”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Times">The Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.thetimes.co.uk/article/modern-manners-zk68s79b78z">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">If the service <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a> and the meal a disaster, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> should withhold a tip and explain why <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> are doing so. Few of us have the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a></b> to do this.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> December 11,  John Scalzi,  “Your Creation Museum Report”, in  <cite>Whatever</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://whatever.scalzi.com/2007/11/12/your-creation-museum-report/">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But seriously, the ability to just come out and put on a placard that the Jurassic era <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> temporally contiguous with the Fifth Dynasty of the Old Kingdom of Egypt — well, there’s a word for that, and that word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Oliver" class="extiw" title="w:John Oliver">John <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a></a>,  “Daily Fantasy Sports”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Last_Week_Tonight_with_John_Oliver" class="extiw" title="w:Last Week Tonight with John Oliver">Last Week Tonight with John <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a></a></cite>, season 2, episode 34, written by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Carvell" class="extiw" title="w:Tim Carvell"><a href = vnd.unilang:tim.html>Tim</a> Carvell</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:josh.html>Josh</a> Gondelman; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dan_Gurewitch" class="extiw" title="w:Dan Gurewitch"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>Dan</a> Gurewitch</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:jeff.html>Jeff</a> Maurer; <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Silva; Will Tracy; <a href = vnd.unilang:jill.html>Jill</a> Twiss; Seena Vali; <a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a> Weiner, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HBO" class="extiw" title="w:HBO">HBO</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros._Television" class="extiw" title="w:Warner Bros. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciano.html>ciano</a> (35261)</h1><br></body> 
***ciao.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a> (10126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Venetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Venetian language">Venetian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">sciavo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in particular the expression <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao vostro</i>, literally meaning "(I am) your slave" but in essence meaning "I am at your service", or "your humble servant"), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sclavus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence also standard Italian <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">schiavo</i>); in the Venetian language originally pronounced <span class="IPA">/stʃaʊ/</span>. Development and use <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to the Southern German and Central European greeting of <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">servus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_6">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a>!</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>hello!
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:salve.html>salve</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:buongiorno.html>buongiorno</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>goodbye!
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="it">arrivederla <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:arrivederci.html>arrivederci</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="it">ci vediamo <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>Early 1940s</b>, written by an unknown Italian partisan, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bella_ciao" class="extiw" title="w:Bella ciao"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bella.html>Bella</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>Ciao</a></i></a> (<i>Goodbye, beautiful!</i>):
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="it">È questo il <a href = vnd.unilang:fiore.html>fiore</a> del partigiano,<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bella.html>bella</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:bella.html>bella</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:bella.html>bella</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a></b>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a></b>!<br /> È questo il <a href = vnd.unilang:fiore.html>fiore</a> del partigiano,<br /> morto per la libertà!</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the flower of the partisan,<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> beautiful, <b>goodbye</b>! Beautiful, <b>goodbye</b>! Beautiful, <b>goodbye</b>, <b>goodbye</b>, <b>goodbye</b>!<br /> This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the flower of the partisan,<br /> Who died for freedom!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***cicero.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a> (19688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From its use in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pannartz_and_Sweynheim" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pannartz and Sweynheim">Pannartz and Sweynheim</a>'s 1467 Roman edition of <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>Cicero</a>'s <i>Epistulae ad Familiares</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> to My Friends").<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ciceros</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Continental  printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Continental equivalent of the English pica: a measure of 12 Didot points (4.51368 mm or about 0.178 in.) or a body of type in this size.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>cicero</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(typografie)</span> typografische <a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drukletter.html>drukletter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 12 <a href = vnd.unilang:punten.html>punten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfer</a> (8862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cifer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cifra</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>digit</li>
<li>statistic</li>
<li>a grade given for an assignment or class, particularly in primary school</li></ol>

***cilinder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cilinder.html>cilinder</a> (17060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cylindre</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cylindrus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roller, cylinder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύλινδρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúlindros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a cylinder, roller, roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>," from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κυλίνδω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kulíndō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cilinder.html>cilinder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cilinders.html>cilinders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cilinder.html>cilindertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cylinder (geometric three-dimensional solid shape)</li>
<li>certain <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> of (roughly) cylindrical shape, e.g. a top hat</li>
<li>cylinder (of an engine)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cilinder.html>cilinder</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***cipier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipier</a> (12480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cepier</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cipiers.html>cipiers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">jailor</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">warden</span>, prison guard
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevangenbewaarder.html>gevangenbewaarder</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevangenisbewaarder.html>gevangenisbewaarder</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg/220px-Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="241" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg/330px-Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg/440px-Carceleros_guatanamo.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1929" data-file-height="2112" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:kunstwerk.html>kunstwerk</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Guatanamo</div></div></div>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:cipier.html>cipier</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***citaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:citaat.html>citaat</a> (10573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">citātum</i>, the neutral inflection of the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">citō</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">citāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cause to move, arouse, summon, urge, call</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the frequentative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cieō</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ciēre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, set in motion, stir, rouse, call, invite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> base <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move to and fro</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: somewhat equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citeren.html>citeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aat</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citaat.html>citaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citaten.html>citaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citaat.html>citaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A quotation, fragment of a human expression, notably as reference</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:citeren.html>citeren</a> (12479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:citer.html>citer</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:citeren.html>citeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quote a text and/or an author</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to summon, subpoena to appear in court</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cite, to make an honorable mention of (someone) in a citation, notably in the military</li></ol>

</p>

***clarion.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:clarion.html>clarion</a> (38440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">claron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clario</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clārus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clarion.html>clarion</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">clarions</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A medieval brass instrument, related to the trumpet, or its sound.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="es">claro</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clarion.html>clarion</a>'</b>s call to action <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A different type of musical instrument resembling an organ.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clarion.html>clarion</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">clarions</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">clarioning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">clarioned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To sound a <a href = vnd.unilang:clarion.html>clarion</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">trumpet-like instrument</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make a similar sound to the instrument.
<ul><li><b>1946</b>, Rebecca Rogers, <i>They Ask for Bread</i> (page 16)
<dl><dd>His deep voice <b>clarioned</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> and he paused, hearing them whisper away into their last faint echoes in the organ loft.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:clausule.html>clausule</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clausula</i>. The stress shift to penultimate by influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:clausule.html>clausule</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:clausule.html>clausule</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:clausules.html>clausules</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:clausule.html>clausuletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A clause, provision, stipulation in a contract, law etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belgische.html>Belgische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verklaart.html>verklaart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheime.html>geheime</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clausules.html>clausules</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:openbare.html>openbare</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clausules.html>clausules</a></b> tenietdoen <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeldig.html>ongeldig</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Belgian law declares secret <b>clauses</b> undoing public <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> invalid.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
